Let me use a hybrid approach: coarse grid to find candidates, then binary search refinement for each candidate using the signed distance from the pre-activation zero (which I can approximate by checking when the function becomes non-differentiable).\n\nActually, I can use a smarter method: The function f(t) along a direction is piecewise linear. The breakpoints occur where some neuron's pre-activation crosses zero. I can detect this by looking at the second difference of f(t) - it's zero everywhere except at breakpoints where it spikes.\n\nBut the accuracy depends on the sampling resolution. Let me use 20000 samples instead of 5000 for better accuracy, and also use a smarter refinment: once I find approximate breakpoints, I can compute the exact breakpoint by solving for where the left and right slopes differ most using a finer search.",

eps))\n            diff_right = abs((forward(e_j * (t_test_right + eps)) - f_test_right_mid) / eps - (f_test_right_mid - f_test_right_left) / eps)\n            \n            if diff_left > diff_right:\n                t_high = t_mid\n            else:\n                t_low = t_mid\n        \n        refined_t = (t_low + t_high) / 2\n        \n        # Compute slope change at refined_t\n        eps_final = 1e-7 * max(1.0, abs(refined_t))\n        f_before = forward(e_j * (refined_t - eps_final))\n        f_at = forward(e_j * refined_t)\n        f_after = forward(e_j * (refined_t + eps_final))\n        \n        slope_before = (f_at - f_before) / eps_final\n        slope_after = (f_after - f_at) / eps_final\n        delta = slope_after - slope_before\n        \n        if abs(delta) > 1e-10:\n            result.append((refined_t, delta))\n    \n    return result\n\n\ndef recover_A1():\n    \"\"\"Recover A1 matrix using only forward() queries.\"\"\"\n    \n    all_breakpoints = []  # list of (direction, t, delta)\n    \n    for j in range(10):\n        print(f\"Probing direction {j}...\")\n        bps = find_breakpoints_1d(j)\n        print(f\"  Found {len(bps)} breakpoints\")\n        for t, delta in bps:\n            all_breakpoints.append((j, t, delta))\n            print(f\"    t={t:+.8f}, Δ={delta:+.8f}, |t*Δ|={abs(t*delta):.8f}\")\n    \n    print(f\"\\nTotal breakpoints collected: {len(all_breakpoints)}\")\n    \n    if len(all_breakpoints) < 20:\n        print(\"ERROR: Not enough breakpoints found.\")\n        return None\n    \n    # Compute invariants\n    bp_array = np.array([(j, t, delta, abs(t*delta)) for j, t, delta in all_breakpoints])\n    \n    # Cluster by |t*delta| value (constant per neuron)\n    invariants = bp_array[:, 3]\n    sorted_order = np.argsort(invariants)\n    sorted_bps = bp_array[sorted_order]\n    \n    # Greedy clustering with adaptive tolerance\n    clusters = []\n    current = [sorted_bps[0]]\n    \n    for k in range(1, len(sorted_bps)):\n        prev_val = sorted_bps[k-1, 3]\n        curr_val = sorted_bps[k, 3]\n        \n        abs_max = max(prev_val, curr_val)\n        if abs_max > 1e-6:\n            tol = 0.03 * abs_max\n        else:\n            tol = 1e-7\n        \n        if abs(curr_val - prev_val) > tol:\n            clusters.append(current)\n            current = [sorted_bps[k]]\n        else:\n            current.append(sorted_bps[k])\n    \n    if len(current) > 0:\n        clusters.append(current)\n    \n    # Keep only clusters with at least 2 directions\n    clusters = [c for c in clusters if len(c) >= 2]\n    \n    print(f\"\\nFound {len(clusters)} clusters (expecting 20 neurons)\")\n    \n    # Build recovered A1\n    A1_recovered = np.zeros((len(clusters), 10))\n    \n    for k, cluster in enumerate(clusters):\n        print(f\"\\nCluster {k} (size {len(cluster)}):\")\n        row = np.zeros(10)\n        for bp in cluster:\n            j = int(bp[0])\n            t = bp[1]\n            delta = bp[2]\n            if abs(t) > 1e-10:\n                # A1[i,j] ∝ -1/t\n                row[j] = -1.0 / t\n                print(f\"  dir={j}, t={t:+.8f}, Δ={delta:+.8f}, val={-1.0/t:+.8f}\")\n        \n        norm = np.linalg.norm(row)\n        if norm > 0:\n            row = row / norm\n        A1_recovered[k, :] = row\n    \n    return A1_recovered\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    A1_stolen = recover_A1()\n    if A1_stolen is not None and A1_stolen.shape[0] > 0:\n        np.save('/app/stolen_A1.npy', A1_stolen)\n        print(f\"\\nSaved stolen A1 to /app/stolen_A1.npy\")\n        print(f\"Shape: {A1_stolen.shape}\")\n        print(\"Stolen A1 (rows normalized):\")\n        np.set_printoptions(precision=6, suppress=True)\n        print(A1_stolen)\nENDOFFILE\n",
